\ul\b\f1\fs28\par
(2) How to sell anything to anyone - sell me this pen\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 1.people buy based on emotions and not by logic\par
eg. wearing  a suit and pretending it to belike james bond as said by sales person\par

\b0 3.pepole dont buy product and services they buy stories (\b FACTS TELL STORIES SELL)\b0\par
( because there is many options available in the market place but if we add emotions to a product which is a story like adding brand adding real time stories to it etc)\par
eg. to sell a 800 dollar pen rather than 20 dollar pen is by adding a stroy like the brand name of 800 dollar pen related to famous personality\par
\ul\b\f1\fs28\par
(3) Stop selling Start Closing (salesman vs closer)\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 *you only get paid by closing and not by selling*\par
Formula :-\b ADD\b0  \b VALUE IN ADVANCE     ,  ADD 10 TIMES MORE VALUE FOR WHAT THEY BUY\par
eg:\b0  If you are teaching a martial arts to a person to reach a black belt , there would be some following steps to reach that so we must provide that steps graphically  and also  \b at that time if you provide a free source which is a streching exercise which is related to the above martial arts but only with that streching exercise you cant get the black belt but help the following first step so this impress a client because we add a free value that helps their actual expectation\par

(6) The Art Of Closing Sales\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 Always prefer two client 1.Hell yes 2.Hell no , Dont prefer the middle one hell\par

while handling hell clients sometimes we can slow down the process of transaction by confirmimg are you comfortable with terms and values etc. and can covert them to intrested client that is to a hell yes client \par
\b FORMULA to be remembered (SW)\line * some will\par
*some wont\par
*so what ?\par
*someone is waiting\par
\b0 never fed up with or try to put over effort with hell no clients !.\ul\b\f1\fs28\par
(7) How To Close A Sale - 5 Reason People Wont Buy\par
\ulnone\f0\fs22 1. No Need / Low Need \par
\b0 (cut away from these type of client)\par
\b 2.No Urgency \par
\b0 (Make a reason for urgency , demonstrate again by adding words limited period offer , right now expectations from industry , if you wont close today you wont close tomorrow etc.)\par
\b 3.No Desire\par
\b0 (create the desire by  doing \b (2) (1) \b0 )\par
\b 4.No Money\par
\b0 (understand wheteher they have money to afford or he/she is person with no money by putforth of some questions like \{eg : you inverst in your car bikes mobile etc. because you trust it suits which is a temporary happiness but why dont you trust yourself for doing a personal inversement which is a permanant happiness \},  if he or she doent have money cut away from those type of client)\par
another example is we can ask them which weights higher VALUE or MONEY\par
\b 5.No Trust\par
\b0 1. people who dont trust us :\par
(give them more social proofs and feedback of coustomers who are happy with your products , history of company , case study , why we prefer them !)\par
2.people who dont trust them :\par
(give them the value that it will not be a waste for client and build the trust)\par
(if they have already on to the product and think it dint suit them give them the difference that you are updated with  than what they had)\f1\fs28\par
\ul\b (8) How To Sell A Product - Sell Anything To Anyone With this Unusual Method\ulnone\b0\par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (9) Top 5 Tips On How To Sell Anything To Anyone :\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 People buy by emotions and justify by logic so understand the painpoint and emotion.Sell the emotions and stroies as said in \b (2)\par
\b0 Start the phone call / meet by telling :\par
Hi Mr.xxxxx , the purpose of this phonecall/meet today is to determine  to see if its a good fit for you and I to work together, by the end of our conversation three things you could say to me 1. yes (we can move forward from there) 2.No( and i want you to know is perfectly okay to say no to me \{if client replies no go back to \b (5) \b0\}). 3. i will think about it ( which is you could say but i dont want you to ) \b PREFRAMING :\b0  so before we start lets go with a agreement whether you could say me yes or no but no the third one isnt that fair . So at the end it becomes difficult for the client  to tell no.\par
BE AN EXPERT that is make the client call you by sending a proposal which urges him to call atleast to know details. So you can have the control of the sale .\par
\b when client is close to closing a sale but he doesnt putforth the questions :\par
\b0 1. is this a question of price or question of value ? (let the client talk)\par
2.There are many options but why are we talking in phone today ?(here we circle the client need and we pinpoint)\par
3. if they tell other companies are cheaper compared to you \par
reply : I can appretiate that , I dont know that our competitors are charging little bit less ,They are always discounting their sevices , Why do you think that they are always dicounting their services ? See the end of the day i think the question is not  about the price but its about the value isnt it? As a person I believe no fees is too high for success and Any fees is always higher for failure.so what we want to do to make sure is to produce  result for you , I want to be a revenue generator a profit centre for you and not an expense ,Does this make a sense ? \b\par
\ul\f1\fs28 (10) The One Secret To Close More Sales On The Phone\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 Make the client call you instead of you call them .BE AN EXPERT that is make the client call you by sending a proposal which urges him to call atleast to know details. So you can have the control of the sale .\par
when we call the client we dont know the exact atmosphere of the client so make them call you , if this is done 50 percent of sales is done , He/she calls because he/she needs the solution for their problem which you have, So here you become the buyer by buying their problem and they become the seller by selling their problem.\par
If the client calls you reply professionally as:\par
1. Hi, this is Ashif , What can i do for you?\par
2. Hi, this is Ashif , What is the deal that you want to make with me today ?\par
NOTE : when you send them the proposal through email make sure it urges them to call you atleast for fetching details ,add your number , name , designation and company name and a schedule link like book a call or schedule a call on _______ time.\par
Need people will schedule so you can filter the worth clients .\par
if this doent work out jump back to \b (9) , \b0  and bring back the control to you as said in \b (10)\par
\ul\f1\fs28 (11) The Three Most Important Skills In Sales\par

eg: if Your prosphet is at a point in career and he want to go to the point in his career there is a gap betwwen those two points , there as a sales peson we must diagnose their problem that our product must be  like a bridge to those two points \par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (12) Client Say How Much Is It? - And You Say\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 when the client ask this they want to get to the bottom -line.\par
So when we give out the price we will loose the sale !.\par
\b 1. So when the client starts with this question\b0  what we have to reply is \b "IT DEPENDS"\par
\b0 So when we reply like this, the client will reply    "It Depends on What?"\par
So we redirect the conversation by replying " It Depends Upon What You Need "\par
so we can know their needs and wants .\par
\b 2. At the end of the conversation if client ask this question :\par
\b0 *Be positive because the client is in idea to buy your product\par
*Tell them the price and continue with the question \b "Are you comfoteable?"\par
"Does this suit your Budget?". \b0 and give some options in payment or product etc.. as said in \b (1)\par
3. If the question is asked in middle of the conversation :\par
\b0 reply by telling like a range (i.e) for eg: it ranges from 10k to 15k \par
\ul\b\f1\fs28 (13) \tab 5 Most Powerful Sales Question Ever\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 Can be used while meeting the client face to face ->  MAJORITY\par
Make sure of your body language and dressing and what outcome you want!.\par
Questions that can be powerful :\par
1. What motivated you to have this meet with us today ? \par
(let the client talk , take notes on what client says)\par
2.\ul Exactly\ulnone  ,what are we trying to accomplish here today ? \ul\b\f1\fs28\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 (let the client talk )\par
3. Where are you today ,and were do you want to be?\par
(now we can understand the pain point of the client and be a bridge as said in \b (11) \b0 )\b\par
\b0 4. what seems to be the problem, and how long are you having this problem ?\par
(we as sales person we can know evrything we want from this question , and understand whether the client is a good fit for us or not)\par
5. If this meeting accomplished everything you could possibly hope for , what would that look like?\par
(this makes a picture in client mind , and they give you the strategy they need )\par
\ul\b\f1\fs28 (14) 5 - persuasive words that controls minds\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 1.YOU ( brings attention that it means them )\par
2.FREE ( attracts easily)\par
3.NEW (updates are prefered by clients always)\par
4.NOW (creates urgency ) eg: available only now , take advantage of the offer now\par
5.SECRET (attracts , excites ,attended,the clients easily)\par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (15) Stupid Questions That Cost You Sales\par
\ulnone\f0\fs22 DONT ASK THESE QUESTIONS\par
\b0 1. How can i help you ? ( this makes the client to think that he is going to be sold)\par
2.Do you have a minute ? ( no slaes can done in a minute its equal to lie)\par
\b (instead use "Is this a Good Time to talk?" )\par
\b0 3. How could you dont want this deal ? (we could not push the client)\par
4.Would you like to have some time to think about it? (Delay kills sales)\par
5.Would you like a proposal or a quote ? (its like chasing behind the client ) -> dont call this and ask\par
6. who is the best salesperson thats ever called you ? (dumb question)\par
7.Can i send you a email ? (proposal or quote) -> try to close the call in phone !\par
8. Are you looking to buy today ? ( people hate to be sold but they love to buy)\par
\b (instead  use "Where should we go from here") -> \ul\fs24 congrats the client after accepting\ulnone\par
\ul\f1\fs28 (16) Client Say "Send Me A Proposal" And You Say :\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 Try to avoid making proposal (its majority a waste of time)\par
Get to the bottom-line and ask \b "I am more happy to send you but ,Exactly what would you hope to see from the proposal? , Lets pretend I send you proposal and you like when you see it , whats gonna happen next ? Are you and I gonna do bussiness ? is that within your budget , I want to find that out early before you write down a single word, I want some kind of financial committment before i do a proposal " \par
\ul\f1\fs28 (17) 4 types of clients :\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 1 . Cheap (eg: starts with how much it cost , compares price with competitors)\par
2.Difficult (eg: I dont have time for this (strictly no clients) )\par
3.Sophisticated  \par
(they know exactly what they want , they are educated and done research on product , so they need time they ask various questions )\par
(eg: i will get back to you before you do , ask features benifits )\par
4.Affluent (buy based on emotions and feelings) \par
(eg: they dont ask much questions so we should not speak much and change their mind)\par
So always deal with SOPHISTICATED AND AFFLUENT clients at majority\par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (18) What to do when your client say no to you\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 Have a downsell (offers , options ) -> that cost them less \par
but the product that you offer with less must be starting stage for the thing that they want \par
eg: if a client wants to move from point A to point D but cannot inverst for that , you can give idea or some support that takes him to move to point B from point A   but not fully to D . So when we do automatically the growth takes to buy D (follow them after some months to know the result)\par
\ul\b\f1\fs28 (19) 6 Ways to Recognize Buying Signals\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 1.client nods his head up and down / touch and see the product \par
(while explaining about the product or while demonstarting)\par
2. When client ask about a specific product \par
(eg: asking about options )\par
3. They use possessive statements\par
(client comments like what would life be like when they have it)\par
(eg: in a furniture showroom , client telling this suits us very well in living room )\par
4.Client asking about price? \par
(asking price in different way how much is it -> its very common)\par
\b but they ask in different way when they want to buy it :\par
* \b0 Is there any finance available ?\par
*Any discounts ?\par
*Is this the best price you could give me?\par
5. when the client ask for start date / delivery ?\par
(eg: when does this starts from)\par
6. when client ask risk minimization question ?\par
(eg: coustomer support , email return , warranty , support systems , return policy)\par
\b they may also ask point 6 if they dont feel comfortable with your product before , so give them the updates that is new than the before product\par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (29) 7 Dumb Questions that cost you money and sales :\par

3. So you are not intrested in my _____ (product) ? (creates resistance between you and client )\par
4. Are you ready to buy today sir/madam? (triggers them that they are gonna be sold for something , pople love to buy but hate to be sold)\par
(instead ask \b Reply : "Where should we go from here ?" /  "What would you like to do next ?") \par
\b0 5. So you actually cant afford to buy this ? (creates conflict between you and client , its like peeping into their financial status)\par
(if money is their problem ask \b Reply : "ummm... what can i do to help you to solve this problem ?") \par
\b0 6. Are you saying you dont have the power to make the decision on your own ? (its an offensive question)\par
7. So. Mr xxxx when should i call you back ? (delay kills sales )\par

\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 1. people based on price (offer price quite less compared to competitor)\par

3. people buy based on quality ( people are of two types they  buy by price on certain product / they buy by quality on certain products )\par
4. people buy based on convinience (because it saves their time)\par
5. people buy because of personalized services ( designed or produced to meet someones individual requirement )\par
\{eg: updat eclient with new product , deliver to them to their place etc.)\par

\ul\b\f1\fs28 (36) The 4 most common buyer types in sales and how to sell to them :\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 the most mistake by sales person is that they treat all clients as same , So qualify the clients and add the value to them as per their qualification.\par
\b 1. Cheap buyers\b0  (they buy based on price but not on value,  they need bundle of things at low price but not quality or value .)\par
\b [so structure your product for cheap buyers based on price ]\par
\b0\{ eg:  have a product is 50 rupees and it is marked up to 80 rupees and shown and finally its on offer we give as 45 rupees , so this satisfy them , this shows them a good deal , create urgency by telling limitted peiod offer. \}\par
\b 2. Difficult Buyers \b0 (they love to fight , they take lot of energy ) -> so better avoid \par
\b 3.Sophisticated buyers \b0 (they are intelligent buyers , they do lot of research )\par
\{what we do is provide information by understanding the needs of client , *and we must tell them what our product wont do *->  this builds trust , discuss also the flaws in our product (eg: the price of our product is higher compared to our competitors because our value is also too high ) -> this to builds trust , dont be pushy , give them space  )\par
\b 4.Affluent buyers \b0 (they buy feelings , emotions , convinince , status) \par
\{eg: we should show them how we could make their life easier , understand the feature , needs , benifits , convinince what the client prefers and have it as your painpoint and closs the sale \} -> they hate inconvinience and they dont want cheap they want best .(we must communicate like \b "This is expensive , this is not for eveyone, and most people probably will not appreciate the beauty of this \b0 (they cannot see the quality in it )\b  , but may be you will ".\par
         \par
                   * so choose your client as (3) and (4) , because choice of client is much important *\par
\b0\par
\ul\b\f1\fs28 (37) How to handle sales objection with the 3 F's method\par
\ulnone\b0\f0\fs22 while talking to  a client and they give you a lot of objections , just do a redirections\par
\b 3 F's Method :\par
*Feel \b0 ( " I understand how you feel")\b\par
*Felt  ("\b0 Others Felt the same way ")\b\par
*Found \b0  ("Here is what I Found")\par
how to use it ( eg: convince a person to take an online course by using above formula)\par
\b Reply : "Yes I understand , Actually I also thought the same on my early stage when I heard this , but when i realized is there are many types of courses available , but when you take the right course based on your needs on well reputed universities, what I found is they give immense career growth and financial growth , because in this competitve world degree with high value is always preferred compared to experience and stuffs. "\par
